1. Dataset 코드 추가
(참고 : https://dsbook.tistory.com/80)
def load_crawling_data():
    import pandas as pd
    from konlpy.tag import Okt
    okt = Okt()
    from gensim.models import Word2Vec
    tokenized_data = []

    print('Loading data...')
    df = pd.read_csv("./data/crawling_data/reviewdata_hotelsdotcom_preprocessed.csv", index_col=[0], nrows=10000)
    df.dropna(subset=['preprocessed_review', 'total_score'], inplace=True)
    data = df['preprocessed_review']
    y = (df['total_score'] / 2)
    y = np.array(y, dtype='int64')
    print(len(data), 'train sequences')

    num_classes = np.max(y)
    print(num_classes, 'classes')

    print('Vectorizing sequence data...')
    for review in data:
        temp = []
        oks = okt.pos(review, join=True)
        for ok in oks:
            text, tag = map(str, ok.split('/'))
            if tag not in ['Josa', 'Eomi', 'Punctation']:
                temp.append(text)
        tokenized_data.append(temp)

    model = Word2Vec(sentences=tokenized_data, window=5, min_count=10, workers=4, sg=1)
    resultfeatureVec = np.zeros((len(tokenized_data), 100), dtype='float32')
    nwords = 0.
    counter = 0.
    idx_to_key = model.wv.index_to_key
    key_to_idx = model.wv.key_to_index
    index2word_set = set(idx_to_key)
    for review in tokenized_data:
        featureVec = np.zeros((100,), dtype='float32')
        for word in review:
            if word in index2word_set:
                nwords = nwords + 1.
                featureVec = np.add(featureVec, model.wv[word])
        featureVec = np.divide(featureVec, nwords)
        # print(featureVec)
        resultfeatureVec[int(counter)] = featureVec
        counter += 1

    # scale to [0,1]
    from sklearn.preprocessing import MinMaxScaler
    x = MinMaxScaler().fit_transform(resultfeatureVec)

    print('x_train shape:', x.shape)
    return x.astype(float), y
